22:06:11 - LLMClient-dashscope - INFO - ğŸ¤– å“åº”å†…å®¹: ```verilog
// Counter Module
// This module implements a configurable WIDTH-bit counter with enable, direction control,
// asynchronous active-low reset, and preset capability.

`timescale 1ns / 1ps

module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Default width is 8 bits
)(
    input           clk,
    input           rst_n,
    input           en,
    input           up,          // Direction control: 1 for up-counting, 0 for down-counting
    input           load,        // Load preset value when asserted
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] preset_value,

    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,
    output reg          full,
    output reg          empty
);

// Purpose: Synchronous counter with configurable direction and load
// Features:
// - Rising edge triggered
// - Asynchronous active-low reset
// - Count direction controlled by 'up' signal
// - Load preset value when 'load' is asserted

always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        // Asynchronous reset (active low)
        count <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        full  <= 1'b0;
        empty <= 1'b1;  // Counter is initially empty
    end
    else if (load) begin
        // Load preset value synchronously
        count <= preset_value;
        // Update status flags based on loaded value
        full  <= (preset_value == {WIDTH{1'b1}});
        empty <= (preset_value == {WIDTH{1'b0}});
    end
    else if (en) begin
        // Only update count when enabled
        if (up) begin
            // Up counter
            count <= count + 1;
            // Update status flags
            full  <= (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}});
            empty <= (count == {WIDTH{1'b0}});
        end
        else begin
            // Down counter
            count <= count - 1;
            // Update status flags
            full  <= (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}});
            empty <= (count == {WIDTH{1'b0}});
        end
    end
    // If not load, not reset, and not enabled, keep current value (no action needed)
end

endmodule
```

## ğŸ“„ ä¼˜åŒ–åçš„Verilogä»£ç å†…å®¹

```verilog
// Counter Module - Area Optimized
// This module implements a parameterized up/down counter with synchronous reset,
// load capability, and direction control.

module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8
)(
    input            clk,
    input            rst_n,
    input            en,
    input            up,
    input            load,
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] preset_value,
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,
    output reg        full,
    output reg        empty
);

// Internal signal for next count value
reg [WIDTH-1:0] next_count;

// Combinational logic for next count value
always @(*) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        next_count = 0;
    end else if (load) begin
        next_count = preset_value;
    end else if (en) begin
        if (up) begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                next_count = 0;
            end else begin
                next_count = count + 1;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == 0) begin
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b1}};
            end else begin
                next_count = count - 1;
            end
        end
    end else begin
        next_count = count;
    end
end

// Sequential logic with synchronous updates
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 0;
        full  <= 1'b0;
        empty <= 1'b1;
    end else begin
        count <= next_count;
        // Update status flags
        full  <= (next_count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) && en && up;
        empty <= (next_count == 0) && en && !up;
    end
end

endmodule
```

### 2. åŸå§‹è®¾è®¡æ–‡ä»¶

## ğŸ“„ ä¼˜åŒ–åçš„Verilogä»£ç å†…å®¹

```verilog
module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8
)(
    input            clk,
    input            rst_n,
    input            en,
    input            up,
    input            load,
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] preset_value,
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,
    output reg        full,
    output reg        empty
);

// Internal signal for next count value
reg [WIDTH-1:0] next_count;

// Combinational logic for next count value
always @(*) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        next_count = 0;
    end else if (load) begin
        next_count = preset_value;
    end else if (en) begin
        if (up) begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                next_count = 0;
            end else begin
                next_count = count + 1;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == 0) begin
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b1}};
            end else begin
                next_count = count - 1;
            end
        end
    end else begin
        next_count = count;
    end
end

// Sequential logic with synchronous updates
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 0;
        full  <= 1'b0;
        empty <= 1'b1;
    end else begin
        count <= next_count;
        // Update status flags
        full  <= (next_count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) && en && up;
        empty <= (next_count == 0) && en && !up;
    end
end

endmodule
```

## ğŸ“Š ä»£ç ä¼˜åŒ–è¯´æ˜

## ğŸ“„ ä¼˜åŒ–åçš„Verilogä»£ç å†…å®¹

```verilog
module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8
)(
    input            clk,
    input            rst_n,
    input            en,
    input            up,
    input            load,
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] preset_value,
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,
    output reg        full,
    output reg        empty
);

// Internal signal for next count value
reg [WIDTH-1:0] next_count;

// Combinational logic for next count value
always @(*) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        next_count = 0;
    end else if (load) begin
        next_count = preset_value;
    end else if (en) begin
        if (up) begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                next_count = 0;
            end else begin
                next_count = count + 1;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == 0) begin
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b1}};
            end else begin
                next_count = count - 1;
            end
        end
    end else begin
        next_count = count;
    end
end

// Sequential logic with synchronous updates
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 0;
        full  <= 1'b0;
        empty <= 1'b1;
    end else begin
        count <= next_count;
        // Update status flags
        full  <= (next_count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) && en && up;
        empty <= (next_count == 0) && en && !up;
    end
end

endmodule
```

```verilog
module counter(
    input      clk,
    input      rst_n,
    input      enable,
    output reg [3:0] count
);

always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 4'b0;
    end else if (enable) begin
        count <= count + 1'b1;
    end
end

endmodule
```

module counter(
    input      clk,
    input      rst_n,
    input      enable,
    output reg [3:0] count
);

always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 4'b0;
    end else if (enable) begin
        count <= count + 1'b1;
    end
end

endmodule

```verilog
module counter(
    input      clk,
    input      rst_n,
    input      enable,
    output reg [3:0] count
);

always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 4'b0;
    end else if (enable) begin
        count <= count + 1'b1;
    end
end

endmodule
```

### âœ… Verilog æµ‹è¯•å°ä»£ç ï¼ˆtestbench.vï¼‰

```verilog
`timescale 1ns/1ps

module tb_counter;

    // ä¿¡å·å£°æ˜
    reg         clk;
    reg         rst_n;
    reg         enable;
    wire [3:0]  count;

    // æµ‹è¯•è®¡æ•°å™¨å˜é‡
    integer passed_count = 0;
    integer failed_count = 0;
    integer total_count = 0;
    integer test_number = 0;
    string  test_name;

    // è¢«æµ‹æ¨¡å—å®ä¾‹åŒ–
    counter uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .rst_n(rst_n),
        .enable(enable),
        .count(count)
    );

    // æ—¶é’Ÿç”Ÿæˆï¼ˆå‘¨æœŸ10nsï¼‰
    always begin
        #5 clk = ~clk;
    end

    // åˆå§‹è¿‡ç¨‹
    initial begin
        integer i;
        reg [3:0] expected;

        // åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¿¡å·
        clk = 0;
        rst_n = 0;
        enable = 0;

        // æ³¢å½¢è½¬å‚¨è®¾ç½®
        $dumpfile("counter_tb.vcd");
        $dumpvars(0, tb_counter);

        // æ˜¾ç¤ºå¼€å§‹ä¿¡æ¯
        $display("Starting counter testbench...");

        // åŸºæœ¬è®¡æ•°æµ‹è¯•
        test_number = test_number + 1;
        test_name = "basic_counting";
        $display("Time=%0t: Test Case %0d - %s", $time, test_number, test_name);

        rst_n = 0;
        enable = 1;
        #10 rst_n = 1; // é‡Šæ”¾å¤ä½

        expected = 4'h0;
        for (i = 0; i < 10; i = i + 1) begin
            #10;
            expected = expected + 1;
            if (count === expected) begin
                $display("Time=%0t: PASS - Expected: %h, Got: %h", $time, expected, count);
                passed_count = passed_count + 1;
            end else begin
                $display("Time=%0t: FAIL - Expected: %h, Got: %h", $time, expected, count);
